@block

// Calculate meters
bscnt > meter_sampletime ? 
(
	peaki1 = ((264 + ((log(peakvoli1) * meter_sc))) / 264) * 21; peaki1 < 0 ? peaki1 = 0 : peaki1 > 21 ? peaki1 = 21;
	peaki2 = ((264 + ((log(peakvoli2) * meter_sc))) / 264) * 21; peaki2 < 0 ? peaki2 = 0 : peaki2 > 21 ? peaki2 = 21;
	peaki3 = ((264 + ((log(peakvoli3) * meter_sc))) / 264) * 21; peaki3 < 0 ? peaki3 = 0 : peaki3 > 21 ? peaki3 = 21;
	peaki4 = ((264 + ((log(peakvoli4) * meter_sc))) / 264) * 21; peaki4 < 0 ? peaki4 = 0 : peaki4 > 21 ? peaki4 = 21;
	peaki5 = ((264 + ((log(peakvoli5) * meter_sc))) / 264) * 21; peaki5 < 0 ? peaki5 = 0 : peaki5 > 21 ? peaki5 = 21;
	peaki6 = ((264 + ((log(peakvoli6) * meter_sc))) / 264) * 21; peaki6 < 0 ? peaki6 = 0 : peaki6 > 21 ? peaki6 = 21;
	peaki7 = ((264 + ((log(peakvoli7) * meter_sc))) / 264) * 21; peaki7 < 0 ? peaki7 = 0 : peaki7 > 21 ? peaki7 = 21;
	peaki8 = ((264 + ((log(peakvoli8) * meter_sc))) / 264) * 21; peaki8 < 0 ? peaki8 = 0 : peaki8 > 21 ? peaki8 = 21;
	bscnt = peakvoli1 = peakvoli2 = peakvoli3 = peakvoli4 = peakvoli5 = peakvoli6 = peakvoli7 = peakvoli8 = 0;
	
	peako1 = ((264 + ((log(peakvolo1) * meter_sc))) / 264) * 21; peako1 < 0 ? peako1 = 0 : peako1 > 21 ? peako1 = 21;
	peako2 = ((264 + ((log(peakvolo2) * meter_sc))) / 264) * 21; peako2 < 0 ? peako2 = 0 : peako2 > 21 ? peako2 = 21;
	peako3 = ((264 + ((log(peakvolo3) * meter_sc))) / 264) * 21; peako3 < 0 ? peako3 = 0 : peako3 > 21 ? peako3 = 21;
	peako4 = ((264 + ((log(peakvolo4) * meter_sc))) / 264) * 21; peako4 < 0 ? peako4 = 0 : peako4 > 21 ? peako4 = 21;
	peako5 = ((264 + ((log(peakvolo5) * meter_sc))) / 264) * 21; peako5 < 0 ? peako5 = 0 : peako5 > 21 ? peako5 = 21;
	peako6 = ((264 + ((log(peakvolo6) * meter_sc))) / 264) * 21; peako6 < 0 ? peako6 = 0 : peako6 > 21 ? peako6 = 21;
	peako7 = ((264 + ((log(peakvolo7) * meter_sc))) / 264) * 21; peako7 < 0 ? peako7 = 0 : peako7 > 21 ? peako7 = 21;
	peako8 = ((264 + ((log(peakvolo8) * meter_sc))) / 264) * 21; peako8 < 0 ? peako8 = 0 : peako8 > 21 ? peako8 = 21;
	bscnt = peakvolo1 = peakvolo2 = peakvolo3 = peakvolo4 = peakvolo5 = peakvolo6 = peakvolo7 = peakvolo8 = 0;
);
bscnt += samplesblock;


// ________________________________________________________________________________________________
// SAMPLE ////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
// ,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,,
// .............................................................................................

@sample

// gain inputs
spi1 = spl0 * slider1;
spi2 = spl1 * slider3;
spi3 = spl2 * slider5;
spi4 = spl3 * slider7;
spi5 = spl4 * slider9;
spi6 = spl5 * slider11;
spi7 = spl6 * slider13;
spi8 = spl7 * slider15;

// mix outputs
spo1 = spo2 = spo3 = spo4 = spo5 = spo6 = spo7 = spo8 = 0;
i1o1 ? spo1 += spi1; i2o1 ? spo1 += spi2; i3o1 ? spo1 += spi3; i4o1 ? spo1 += spi4; i5o1 ? spo1 += spi5; i6o1 ? spo1 += spi6; i7o1 ? spo1 += spi7; i8o1 ? spo1 += spi8;
i1o2 ? spo2 += spi1; i2o2 ? spo2 += spi2; i3o2 ? spo2 += spi3; i4o2 ? spo2 += spi4; i5o2 ? spo2 += spi5; i6o2 ? spo2 += spi6; i7o2 ? spo2 += spi7; i8o2 ? spo2 += spi8;
i1o3 ? spo3 += spi1; i2o3 ? spo3 += spi2; i3o3 ? spo3 += spi3; i4o3 ? spo3 += spi4; i5o3 ? spo3 += spi5; i6o3 ? spo3 += spi6; i7o3 ? spo3 += spi7; i8o3 ? spo3 += spi8;
